  <content type="text/html">&lt;b&gt;A few new features for the Google Buzz API.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Blog post:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&quot; &gt;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This update includes:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A &amp;quot;garden hose&amp;quot; feed&lt;/b&gt; — a sampled version of the PubSubHubbub-enabled firehose, for testing and development purposes.  (The full firehose is still available for free, of course — but we noticed a number of people wanted to build apps on Google App Engine, and this will fit under the free-to-get-started limits on GAE.)&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A people search by activity API&lt;/b&gt; (with geolocation!) — a geo and topic filtered search for people.  Uses Portable Contacts.  Super cool.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A related Buzz API&lt;/b&gt; — find related Buzz posts for any given Buzz post.  (How awesome is that?)&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The docs will be up in a minute over at:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&quot; &gt;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Be sure to read the blog post for more details and examples.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Enjoy!</content>

   <content type="html">&lt;b&gt;A few new features for the Google Buzz API.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Blog post:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&quot; &gt;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This update includes:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A &amp;quot;garden hose&amp;quot; feed&lt;/b&gt; — a sampled version of the PubSubHubbub-enabled firehose, for testing and development purposes.  (The full firehose is still available for free, of course — but we noticed a number of people wanted to build apps on Google App Engine, and this will fit under the free-to-get-started limits on GAE.)&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A people search by activity API&lt;/b&gt; (with geolocation!) — a geo and topic filtered search for people.  Uses Portable Contacts.  Super cool.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A related Buzz API&lt;/b&gt; — find related Buzz posts for any given Buzz post.  (How awesome is that?)&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The docs will be up in a minute over at:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&quot; &gt;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Be sure to read the blog post for more details and examples.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Enjoy!</content>

  <content type="text/html">&lt;b&gt;A few new features for the Google Buzz API.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Blog post:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&quot; &gt;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This update includes:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A &amp;quot;garden hose&amp;quot; feed&lt;/b&gt; — a sampled version of the PubSubHubbub-enabled firehose, for testing and development purposes.  (The full firehose is still available for free, of course — but we noticed a number of people wanted to build apps on Google App Engine, and this will fit under the free-to-get-started limits on GAE.)&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A people search by activity API&lt;/b&gt; (with geolocation!) — a geo and topic filtered search for people.  Uses Portable Contacts.  Super cool.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A related Buzz API&lt;/b&gt; — find related Buzz posts for any given Buzz post.  (How awesome is that?)&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The docs will be up in a minute over at:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&quot; &gt;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Be sure to read the blog post for more details and examples.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Enjoy!</content>

   <content type="html">&lt;b&gt;A few new features for the Google Buzz API.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Blog post:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&quot; &gt;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This update includes:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A &amp;quot;garden hose&amp;quot; feed&lt;/b&gt; — a sampled version of the PubSubHubbub-enabled firehose, for testing and development purposes.  (The full firehose is still available for free, of course — but we noticed a number of people wanted to build apps on Google App Engine, and this will fit under the free-to-get-started limits on GAE.)&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A people search by activity API&lt;/b&gt; (with geolocation!) — a geo and topic filtered search for people.  Uses Portable Contacts.  Super cool.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A related Buzz API&lt;/b&gt; — find related Buzz posts for any given Buzz post.  (How awesome is that?)&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The docs will be up in a minute over at:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&quot; &gt;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Be sure to read the blog post for more details and examples.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Enjoy!</content>

  <content type="text/html">&lt;b&gt;A few new features for the Google Buzz API.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Blog post:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&quot; &gt;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This update includes:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A &amp;quot;garden hose&amp;quot; feed&lt;/b&gt; — a sampled version of the PubSubHubbub-enabled firehose, for testing and development purposes.  (The full firehose is still available for free, of course — but we noticed a number of people wanted to build apps on Google App Engine, and this will fit under the free-to-get-started limits on GAE.)&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A people search by activity API&lt;/b&gt; (with geolocation!) — a geo and topic filtered search for people.  Uses Portable Contacts.  Super cool.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A related Buzz API&lt;/b&gt; — find related Buzz posts for any given Buzz post.  (How awesome is that?)&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The docs will be up in a minute over at:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&quot; &gt;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Be sure to read the blog post for more details and examples.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Enjoy!</content>

   <content type="html">&lt;b&gt;A few new features for the Google Buzz API.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Blog post:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&quot; &gt;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This update includes:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A &amp;quot;garden hose&amp;quot; feed&lt;/b&gt; — a sampled version of the PubSubHubbub-enabled firehose, for testing and development purposes.  (The full firehose is still available for free, of course — but we noticed a number of people wanted to build apps on Google App Engine, and this will fit under the free-to-get-started limits on GAE.)&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A people search by activity API&lt;/b&gt; (with geolocation!) — a geo and topic filtered search for people.  Uses Portable Contacts.  Super cool.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A related Buzz API&lt;/b&gt; — find related Buzz posts for any given Buzz post.  (How awesome is that?)&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The docs will be up in a minute over at:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&quot; &gt;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Be sure to read the blog post for more details and examples.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Enjoy!</content>

  <content type="text/html">&lt;b&gt;A few new features for the Google Buzz API.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Blog post:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&quot; &gt;http://googlecode.blogspot.com/2010/08/new-google-buzz-api-features-including.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This update includes:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A &amp;quot;garden hose&amp;quot; feed&lt;/b&gt; — a sampled version of the PubSubHubbub-enabled firehose, for testing and development purposes.  (The full firehose is still available for free, of course — but we noticed a number of people wanted to build apps on Google App Engine, and this will fit under the free-to-get-started limits on GAE.)&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A people search by activity API&lt;/b&gt; (with geolocation!) — a geo and topic filtered search for people.  Uses Portable Contacts.  Super cool.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;b&gt;A related Buzz API&lt;/b&gt; — find related Buzz posts for any given Buzz post.  (How awesome is that?)&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The docs will be up in a minute over at:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;　&lt;a href=&quot;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&quot; &gt;http://code.google.com/apis/buzz/v1/using_rest.html&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Be sure to read the blog post for more details and examples.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Enjoy!</content>
